msg:The hotel design is great, the facilities are complete, and the newly built hotels are relatively new. It is next to the Xinshi Ancient Town Scenic Area, and it is very convenient to visit the ancient town. Next to the hotel is the Beijing-Hangzhou Grand Canal. There were many guests during the May Day holiday, and the hotel was crowded and a bit noisy. I stayed in Building 2, and the terrace faced the hotel. The privacy is not good, and the guests are noisy at night. If you have the conditions, I recommend staying in Building 5, Building 3, and Building 1. The hotel buffet looks very rich. The taste is average. I went to the barbecue iron plate three or four times and didn't get anything once. The chef said that people are more mixed now. I think those who consume in your place are guests, and they all pay for room and food. Why are they divided into three, six, and nine levels? The hotel parking lot is not big, and the underground parking is estimated to be able to hold more than 100 vehicles. When I saw that I had a license plate from another province, I was directly asked to park in the temporary parking lot. It took about ten minutes to walk. The vehicles from the province before and after me were allowed to go to the basement. I hope this is just an occasional phenomenon, don't treat them differently. After all, there are not too many people on May Day. Such a new hotel can't even solve the parking problem now.
